Source Code

This source code is very close to the Apollo Guidance Computer software for the Apollo 13 Lunar module. This revision of the Luminary 131 program is from December of 1969, whereas there was a later revision in January of 1970, and still another revision in February, which is the code that flew on the mission. As far as this transcription is concerned, it was originally from a copy made in 1991 of a printout from the collection of AGC developer Don Eyles for collector David Craig. It was subsequently scanned by Gary Neff, reprocessed for online presentation at the now-discontinued History of Recent Science and Technology (HRST) website of MIT's Dibner Institute (the full-quality scans being discarded in the process), and finally transcribed by Ron Burkey for the Virtual AGC Project. Although a high-quality replacement scan for a completely illegible page was later provided by Gary Neff, the reduced legibility of the reprocessed HRST posting nevertheless caused many errors to be introduced into the transcription. Accordingly, a second scan of the same physical printout was made in 2017 for the Virtual AGC Project's collection at the Internet Archive, and used to correct the transcription errors. All of the scanned materials mentioned, as well as other Luminary 131 related material, are available online. Don Eyles apprently made additional hand-written notes in printout between 1991 and 2017, so the two scans are not identical in that respect. The page-headings in the printout read, in part:
	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 131 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-091
	17:53 DEC. 19, 1969
Note that the date is the date the printout was made, not the date on which the program revision was released, although these happen to be very close together. 

021020,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
021021,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
021022,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary 1C, revision 131.
021023,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
021024,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13.
021025,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
021026,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
021027,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the 
021028,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
021029,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 496-618
021030,000012:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.

021048,000030:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021049,000031: 
021050,000032:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021051,000033: 
021052,000034:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021053,000035:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021054,000036: 
021055,000037:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021056,000038: 
021057,000039:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021058,000040:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021059,000041:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021060,000042:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021061,000043: 
021062,000044:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021063,000045: 
021064,000046:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021065,000047: 
021066,000048:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021067,000049: 
021068,000050:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021069,000051:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021070,000052:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021071,000053:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021072,000054:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021073,000055:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021074,000056:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021075,000057:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021076,000058:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021077,000059:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021078,000060: 
021079,000061:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021080,000062: 
021081,000063:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021082,000064:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021083,000065: 
021084,000066:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021085,000067: 
021086,000068:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021087,000069: 
021088,000070:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021089,000071: 
021090,000072:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021091,000073: 
021092,000074:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021093,000075: 
021094,000076:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021095,000077: 
021096,000078:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
021097,000079: 
021098,000080:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021099,000081: 
021100,000082:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
021101,000083: 
021102,000084: 25,2073  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.

021516,000498:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021517,000499: 
021518,000500:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021519,000501:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021520,000502:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021521,000503: 
021522,000504:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021523,000505: 
021524,000506:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021525,000507:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021526,000508:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021527,000509:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021528,000510: 
021529,000511:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021530,000512: 
021531,000513:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E

021605,000587:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021606,000588:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021607,000589: 
021608,000590:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021609,000591:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021610,000592: 
021611,000593:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021612,000594: 
021613,000595:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021614,000596:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021615,000597: 
021616,000598:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021617,000599: 
021618,000600:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021619,000601:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021620,000602: 
021621,000603:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021622,000604: 
021623,000605:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021624,000606:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021625,000607:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021626,000608: 
021627,000609:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021628,000610: 
021629,000611:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE, UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA

Page 512 

021825,000807:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021826,000808:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021827,000809: 
021828,000810:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021829,000811:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021830,000812: 
021831,000813:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021832,000814: 
021833,000815:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021834,000816:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021835,000817: 
021836,000818:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021837,000819: 
021838,000820:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021839,000821:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021840,000822: 
021841,000823:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021842,000824: 
021843,000825:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021844,000826:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021845,000827:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021846,000828:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021847,000829: 
021848,000830:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021849,000831:                                                                                                  #        
021850,000832:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021851,000833:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021852,000834: 
021853,000835:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021854,000836: 
021855,000837:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021856,000838:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021857,000839:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021858,000840: 
021859,000841:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021860,000842: 
021861,000843:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021862,000844: 
021863,000845:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021864,000846: 
021865,000847:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021866,000848: 
021867,000849:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021868,000850: 
021869,000851:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021870,000852: 
021871,000853:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021872,000854: 
021873,000855:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRSESSM
021874,000856: 
021875,000857: 24,2675  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021876,000858: 24,2675                                           COUNT*   $$/R21

021878,000860: 24,2676           00006                           EXTEND

022051,001033:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022052,001034:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022053,001035: 
022054,001036:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022055,001037:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022056,001038: 
022057,001039:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022058,001040: 
022059,001041:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022060,001042: 
022061,001043:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022062,001044: 
022063,001045:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022064,001046: 
022065,001047:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022066,001048: 
022067,001049:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022068,001050:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022069,001051: 
022070,001052:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022071,001053: 
022072,001054:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1      ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022073,001055:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022074,001056:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 + P20
022075,001057: 
022076,001058:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022077,001059: 
022078,001060:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022079,001061: 
022080,001062:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022081,001063: 
022082,001064:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022083,001065: 
022084,001066:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED -
022085,001067: 
022086,001068:                                                                                                  #        ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
022087,001069: 
022088,001070: 24,3137     1142                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
022089,001071: 24,3137                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
022090,001072: 24,3137           05504        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
022091,001073: 24,3140           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON

022094,001076: 24,3143           40141                           CADR     SETMINDB

022135,001117:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022136,001118:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022137,001119: 
022138,001120:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022139,001121:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022140,001122: 
022141,001123:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022142,001124: 
022143,001125:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022144,001126:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022145,001127:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022146,001128: 
022147,001129:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022148,001130: 
022149,001131:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022150,001132:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022151,001133:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022152,001134:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022153,001135: 
022154,001136:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022155,001137: 
022156,001138:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022157,001139:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022158,001140:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022159,001141: 
022160,001142:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022161,001143: 
022162,001144:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022163,001145:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022164,001146:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022165,001147: 
022166,001148:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022167,001149: 
022168,001150:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022169,001151: 
022170,001152:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022171,001153: 
022172,001154:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022173,001155: 
022174,001156:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022175,001157: 
022176,001158:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022177,001159: 
022178,001160:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022179,001161: 
022180,001162:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022181,001163: 
022182,001164: 24,3210  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022183,001165: 24,3210                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022184,001166: 24,3210           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022185,001167: 24,3211           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022186,001168: 24,3212           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022187,001169: 24,3213           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022188,001170: 24,3214           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022189,001171: 24,3215           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022190,001172: 24,3216           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022191,001173: 24,3217           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022192,001174: 24,3220           05353        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022193,001175: 24,3221           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
022194,001176: 24,3222           33255                           CAF      V16N80                                
022195,001177: 24,3223           04616                           TC       BANKCALL

022251,001233:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM

022480,001462:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022481,001463: 
022482,001464:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022483,001465: 
022484,001466:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022485,001467:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022486,001468:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022487,001469:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022488,001470:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022489,001471: 
022490,001472:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022491,001473:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022492,001474:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022493,001475:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022494,001476: 
022495,001477:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022496,001478:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022497,001479:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022498,001480:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022499,001481:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022500,001482: 
022501,001483:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022502,001484: 
022503,001485:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022504,001486:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022505,001487: 
022506,001488:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022507,001489: 
022508,001490:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022509,001491:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022510,001492:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022511,001493: 
022512,001494:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022513,001495: 
022514,001496:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022515,001497: 
022516,001498:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022517,001499: 
022518,001500:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022519,001501:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)

022564,001546:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                 . IF EITHER:
022565,001547: 
022566,001548:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022567,001549:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.              HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022568,001550:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022569,001551:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022570,001552:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022571,001553:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022572,001554:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022573,001555:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022574,001556:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022575,001557:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022576,001558:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022577,001559:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022578,001560:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022579,001561:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022580,001562:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022581,001563:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU'S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022582,001564:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022583,001565:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022584,001566:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022585,001567:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL

022636,001618:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022637,001619: 
022638,001620:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022639,001621: 
022640,001622:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022641,001623:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022642,001624:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022643,001625:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022644,001626:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022645,001627:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022646,001628:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022647,001629:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022648,001630:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022649,001631:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022650,001632:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022651,001633:                                                                                                  #        TC TASKOVER.
022652,001634: 
022653,001635:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022654,001636:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022655,001637:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022656,001638: 
022657,001639:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022658,001640: 
022659,001641:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022660,001642: 
022661,001643:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022662,001644: 
022663,001645:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022664,001646:                                                                                                  #        
022665,001647:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022666,001648: 
022667,001649:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022668,001650:

022671,001653: 24,3256                                           BANK     24

022685,001667:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022686,001668: 
022687,001669:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022688,001670: 
022689,001671:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022690,001672:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022691,001673:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022692,001674:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022693,001675:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022694,001676:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022695,001677:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU'S
022696,001678:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022697,001679:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022698,001680:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022699,001681:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022700,001682:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022701,001683:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022702,001684:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022703,001685:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022704,001686: 
022705,001687:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022706,001688: 
022707,001689:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022708,001690: 
022709,001691:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022710,001692: 
022711,001693:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022712,001694: 
022713,001695:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_

022716,001698: 
022717,001699:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022718,001700: 
022719,001701:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022720,001702:

022724,001706: 25,2105           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.

022762,001744:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022763,001745: 
022764,001746:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022765,001747: 
022766,001748:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022767,001749:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INIITALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022768,001750:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022769,001751:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022770,001752:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022771,001753:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022772,001754:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022773,001755:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022774,001756:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022775,001757:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022776,001758:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022777,001759:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022778,001760:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022779,001761:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022780,001762:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022781,001763:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022782,001764:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022783,001765:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022784,001766:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022785,001767:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022786,001768:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022787,001769:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022788,001770: 
022789,001771:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022790,001772: 
022791,001773:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022792,001774:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022793,001775: 
022794,001776:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022795,001777: 
022796,001778:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022797,001779: 
022798,001780:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022799,001781: 
022800,001782:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022801,001783: 
022802,001784:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022803,001785: 
022804,001786:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022805,001787: 
022806,001788:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022807,001789: 
022808,001790:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
022809,001791:

022811,001793:

022855,001837:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                 IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022856,001838: 
022857,001839:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                               S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022858,001840:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022859,001841:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022860,001842:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022861,001843:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022862,001844:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022863,001845:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022864,001846:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022865,001847:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022866,001848:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022867,001849:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022868,001850:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022869,001851:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022870,001852:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022871,001853:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022872,001854:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022873,001855:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022874,001856:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022875,001857:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022876,001858:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022877,001859: 
022878,001860:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022879,001861: 
022880,001862:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022881,001863:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022882,001864:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022883,001865:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022884,001866: 
022885,001867:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022886,001868: 
022887,001869:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022888,001870: 
022889,001871:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022890,001872: 
022891,001873:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
022892,001874: 
022893,001875:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022894,001876: 
022895,001877:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022896,001878: 
022897,001879:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022898,001880:

022951,001933:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022952,001934: 
022953,001935:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022954,001936: 
022955,001937:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022956,001938:                                                                                                  #        RRMANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
022957,001939:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022958,001940:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
022959,001941:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
022960,001942:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022961,001943:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022962,001944:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
022963,001945:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022964,001946:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
022965,001947:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022966,001948:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022967,001949:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022968,001950:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
022969,001951: 
022970,001952:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022971,001953:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
022972,001954:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
022973,001955:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022974,001956:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022975,001957: 
022976,001958:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022977,001959: 
022978,001960:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
022979,001961: 
022980,001962:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022981,001963: 
022982,001964:                                                                                                  #        FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
022983,001965: 
022984,001966:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022985,001967: 
022986,001968:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022987,001969: 
022988,001970:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022989,001971: 
022990,001972:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_ REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
022991,001973:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)
022992,001974:                                                                                                  #        L+1 (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)
022993,001975:

023043,002025:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023044,002026: 
023045,002027:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023046,002028: 
023047,002029:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023048,002030:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023049,002031:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023050,002032:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023051,002033:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023052,002034:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023053,002035:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023054,002036:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023055,002037:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023056,002038:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023057,002039:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023058,002040:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023059,002041:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023060,002042: 
023061,002043:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023062,002044:                                                                                                  #        
023063,002045:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023064,002046:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

023153,002135:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023154,002136: 
023155,002137:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023156,002138: 
023157,002139:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023158,002140:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023159,002141:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023160,002142:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023161,002143:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023162,002144:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023163,002145:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023164,002146:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023165,002147:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023166,002148:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023167,002149:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023168,002150:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023169,002151:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023170,002152:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023171,002153:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023172,002154:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023173,002155:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023174,002156:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023175,002157:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023176,002158:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023177,002159:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023178,002160:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023179,002161: 
023180,002162:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023181,002163: 
023182,002164:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023183,002165:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
023184,002166:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023185,002167:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023186,002168: 
023187,002169:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023188,002170: 
023189,002171:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023190,002172: 
023191,002173:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023192,002174: 
023193,002175:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023194,002176:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023195,002177: 
023196,002178:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023197,002179: 
023198,002180:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023199,002181: 
023200,002182:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023201,002183: 
023202,002184:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023203,002185:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
023204,002186:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                 CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
023205,002187:

023243,002225:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023244,002226: 
023245,002227:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023246,002228:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023247,002229:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023248,002230:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023249,002231:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023250,002232:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023251,002233:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023252,002234:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023253,002235:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023254,002236:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023255,002237:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023256,002238:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
023257,002239:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023258,002240:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023259,002241:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023260,002242:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023261,002243:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023262,002244:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023263,002245:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023264,002246:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023265,002247:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
