023416,002398:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023417,002399: 
023418,002400:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023419,002401:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023420,002402:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023421,002403:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023422,002404:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023423,002405:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023424,002406:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023425,002407:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023426,002408:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023427,002409:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023428,002410:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023429,002411:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023430,002412:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023431,002413:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023432,002414:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023433,002415:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023434,002416:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023435,002417:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023436,002418:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023437,002419:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023438,002420:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023439,002421:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023440,002422:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023441,002423:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023442,002424:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023443,002425:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023444,002426: 
023445,002427:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023446,002428: 
023447,002429:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023448,002430:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023449,002431:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023450,002432: 
023451,002433:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023452,002434:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023453,002435: 
023454,002436:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023455,002437:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR, FINDMAC
023456,002438: 
023457,002439:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023458,002440: 
023459,002441:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023460,002442:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023461,002443: 
023462,002444:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023463,002445:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023464,002446:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023465,002447: 
023466,002448: 25,2604           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023511,002493:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023512,002494: 
023513,002495:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023514,002496: 
023515,002497:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023516,002498:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023517,002499:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023518,002500:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023519,002501:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023520,002502:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023521,002503:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023522,002504:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023523,002505:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023524,002506:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023525,002507:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023526,002508:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023527,002509:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023528,002510:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023529,002511:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023530,002512:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023531,002513:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023532,002514:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023533,002515:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023534,002516:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023535,002517:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023536,002518:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023537,002519:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023538,002520:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023539,002521:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023540,002522:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023541,002523:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023542,002524:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023543,002525:                                                                                                  #        CALLED.  IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023544,002526:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023545,002527:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023546,002528:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023547,002529:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023548,002530:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023549,002531:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023550,002532:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023551,002533:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023552,002534: 
023553,002535:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023554,002536: 
023555,002537:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023556,002538: 
023557,002539:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023558,002540: 
023559,002541:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023560,002542:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023561,002543: 
023562,002544:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023563,002545: 
023564,002546:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

Page 552 

023566,002548: 
023567,002549:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023568,002550: 
023569,002551:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023570,002552: 
023571,002553:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023572,002554: 
023573,002555:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023574,002556: 
023575,002557: 25,2646           00006        DODES              EXTEND

023629,002611:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS POINT WE HAVE A ROTATION VECTOR IN DISH AXES LYING IN THE TS PLANE.  CONVERT THIS TO A
023630,002612:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDED RATE AND ENABLE THE TRACKER IF WE ARE WITHIN .5 DEGREES OF THE TARGET.

023636,002618: 25,2731           40110                           CS       RADMODES                              #  A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES POLARITY OF
023637,002619: 25,2732           74740                           MASK     BIT12                                 #  THE SHAFT COMMANDS IN MODE 2 SO THAT A
023638,002620: 25,2733           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  POSITIVE TORQUE APPLIED TO THE SHAFT
023639,002621: 25,2734           12737                           BZF      +3                                    #  GYRO CAUSES A POSITIVE CHANGE IN THE

024377,003359:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024378,003360:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
024379,003361: 
024380,003362:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024381,003363:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024382,003364:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024383,003365:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024384,003366:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024385,003367: 
024386,003368:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024387,003369: 
024388,003370:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024389,003371:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          LPS20.1
024390,003372:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
024391,003373:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
024392,003374:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
024393,003375: 
024394,003376:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024395,003377: 
024396,003378:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024397,003379:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024398,003380:                                                                                                  #        00002 - ERROR EXIT 2 - RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024399,003381: 
024400,003382:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 - COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024401,003383:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024402,003384: 
024403,003385:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) - A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024404,003386:                                                                                                  #        RM - THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024405,003387: 
024406,003388:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024407,003389:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM - THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024408,003390:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN - RR TRUNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024409,003391:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT - RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024410,003392:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,ADG - THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS
024411,003393:                                                                                                  #                MKTIME - THE TIME OF THE RR READING, DP, IN CENTISECONDS
024412,003394: 
024413,003395:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024414,003396:                                                                                                  #        RNRAD, THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 575 

024416,003398:                                                                                                  #                1) RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
024417,003399:                                                                                                  #                2) RR RANGE RATE, SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
024418,003400:                                                                                                  #        THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX, CDUY, CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
024419,003401: 
024420,003402:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  LRS22.1X, A, L, Q, PUSHLIST

024550,003532:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LRS22.2 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 2)
024551,003533:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P VOLANTE  SDC              DATE   4-11-67
024552,003534: 
024553,003535:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
024554,003536:                                                                                                  #        2)  CHECKS IF THE RR LOS (I.E. THE RADAR BORESIGHT VECTOR) IS WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF THE LM +Z AXIS
024555,003537: 
024556,003538:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.2
024557,003539: 
024558,003540:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:  G+N, AUTO   SETMAXDB
024559,003541: 
024560,003542:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT - RETURN TO CALLER WITH MPAC SET TO +0 (VIA SWRETURN)
024561,003543: 
024562,003544:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXIT -  RETURN TO CALLER WITH MPAC SET TO 00001 - RADAR LOS NOT WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF LM +Z AXIS
024563,003545: 
024564,003546:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS - NONE                                                 IN THE AUTO MODE
024565,003547: 
024566,003548:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED -
024567,003549:                                                                                                  #        RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR - A HALF UNIT VECTOR COMPUTED BY LRS22.1
024568,003550:                                                                                                  #        RM - RR RANGE, METERS B-29, FROM LRS22.1
024569,003551:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 CHANNEL 31 - INDICATES AUTOPILOT IS IN AUTO MODE
024570,003552: 
024571,003553:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS - A,L,Q MPAC - PUSHLIST AND PUSHLOC ARE NOT CHANGED BY THIS ROUTINE

024601,003583:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024602,003584:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION - P20-25
024603,003585:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                    ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024604,003586: 
024605,003587:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024606,003588:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024607,003589:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024608,003590:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024609,003591: 
024610,003592:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024611,003593:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024612,003594:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024613,003595:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024614,003596:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024615,003597:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024616,003598:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024617,003599: 
024618,003600:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024619,003601:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024620,003602:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024621,003603: 
024622,003604:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024623,003605:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024624,003606:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024625,003607:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024626,003608:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024627,003609:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024628,003610: 
024629,003611:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024630,003612:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024631,003613:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024632,003614:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024633,003615:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024634,003616:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024635,003617:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024636,003618:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024637,003619:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024638,003620:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024639,003621:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN ACG
024640,003622:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024641,003623:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024642,003624:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024643,003625:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024644,003626: 
024645,003627:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024646,003628:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024647,003629:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

025038,004020: 
025039,004021:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025040,004022:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025041,004023:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025042,004024:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025043,004025: 
025044,004026:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025045,004027:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
025046,004028:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
025047,004029: 
025048,004030:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025049,004031:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025050,004032:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025051,004033:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025052,004034:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025053,004035:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX

Page 589 

025055,004037: 
025056,004038:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025057,004039:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025058,004040:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
025059,004041:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025060,004042:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025061,004043:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025062,004044:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
025063,004045: 
025064,004046: 26,3200           77624        LSR22.4            CALL

025069,004051: 26,3205           77624                           CALL

025171,004153:                                                                                                  #  GETULC
025172,004154:

025200,004182:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
025201,004183: 
025202,004184:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY

025263,004245:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025264,004246:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0                     BY P VOLANTE  SDC               DATE 1-15-67
025265,004247: 
025266,004248:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025267,004249: 
025268,004250:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025269,004251:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025270,004252:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025271,004253:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025272,004254: 
025273,004255:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025274,004256: 
025275,004257:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025276,004258: 
025277,004259:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM
025278,004260:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC        RRDESSM
025279,004261:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
025280,004262:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
025281,004263:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
025282,004264: 
025283,004265:                                                                                                  #  EXIT - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025284,004266: 
025285,004267:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025286,004268: 
025287,004269:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD (SP) - FOR DISPLAY IN R1 -     00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
025288,004270:                                                                                                  #                                                11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
025289,004271:                                                                                                  #        OMEGAD (SP)   - FOR DISPLAY IN R2 -     ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGNT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
025290,004272: 
025291,004273:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025292,004274: 
025293,004275:                                                                                                  #        SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
025294,004276:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
025295,004277: 
025296,004278:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025297,004279: 
025298,004280:                                                                                                  #        RLMSRCH         UXVECT
025299,004281:                                                                                                  #        VXRLM           UYVECT
025300,004282:                                                                                                  #        LOSDESRD        NSRCHPNT
025301,004283:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD        OMEGAD
025302,004284:                                                                                                  #        MPAC            PUSHLIST
025303,004285: 
025304,004286: 26,3442                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
025305,004287: 26,3442           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO                                  
025306,004288: 26,3443           55736                           TS       NSRCHPNT                              #  SET SEARCH PATTERN POINT COUNTER TO ZERO
025307,004289: 26,3444           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
025308,004290: 26,3445           00006                           EXTEND

025313,004295: 26,3451           00006                           EXTEND

025516,004498:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025517,004499:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025518,004500: 
025519,004501:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025520,004502: 
025521,004503:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025522,004504:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025523,004505:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025524,004506:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025525,004507:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025526,004508:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025527,004509: 
025528,004510:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025529,004511: 
025530,004512:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025531,004513: 
025532,004514:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025533,004515:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025534,004516:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025535,004517:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025536,004518:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025537,004519:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025538,004520: 
025539,004521:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025540,004522: 
025541,004523:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025542,004524: 
025543,004525:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025544,004526:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025545,004527:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025546,004528:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025547,004529:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 600 

025549,004531: 
025550,004532:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025551,004533: 
025552,004534:                                                                                                  #        NCR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025553,004535:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025554,004536:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025555,004537:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025556,004538: 
025557,004539:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025558,004540: 
025559,004541:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 10)
025560,004542:                                                                                                  #        LOSSM           LOSVDT/4                (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
025561,004543:                                                                                                  #        SAVECDUT        OLDESFLG                (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
025562,004544:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        READRFLG
025563,004545: 
025564,004546:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
025565,004547: 
025566,004548:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
025567,004549: 
025568,004550:                                                                                                  #        INITIALIZING, IF RR IS FOUND TO BE IN MODE 1:  JOB R29REMOJ AND TASK REMODE:  ALWAYS: TASK PREPOS29.

025570,004552:                                                                                                  #        RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.

025672,004654:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS THAT THE DESIGNATION IS READY FOR NEW DATA.  SETTING LOSCMFLG MAKES IT GO AWAY SO SETUP29D CAN

Page 605 

025745,004727:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025746,004728: 
025747,004729:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025748,004730:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025749,004731:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025750,004732:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025751,004733:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025752,004734: 
025753,004735:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025754,004736:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025755,004737: 
025756,004738: 32,2550                                           BANK     32                                    
025757,004739: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025758,004740: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025759,004741: 
025760,004742: 32,2550                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025761,004743: 32,2550  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025762,004744: 
025763,004745: 32,2550           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025764,004746: 32,2551           55106                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025765,004747: 32,2552           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025766,004748: 
025767,004749: 32,2553           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025768,004750: 32,2554           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025769,004751: 32,2555           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025770,004752: 32,2556           12564                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025771,004753:
